            <div class="scoring-header">

                        <div class="button-group">

                            <a v-bind:href="tournament.ScheduleLink" v-if="!tournament.HideSchedule" class="button-rail">{{tournament.ScheduleLinkText}}</a>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
            <div class="scoring-content" v-for="(match, index) in tournament.Matches" v-if="match.RailPosition!==null" v-bind:style="{order: match.RailPosition}">

                                                            <h2 v-if="match.TeamTieResults.RoundRobinGroupName !== '' && match.TeamTieResults.RoundRobinGroupName.includes('Group')"
                                                            class="rr-city-name">{{match.TeamTieResults.RoundRobinCityName}} - {{match.TeamTieResults.RoundRobinGroupName}}</h2>
